! Title: AdBlock DNS Lite
! Description: 适用于AdGuard的去广告合并规则，每8个小时更新一次。规则源：1Hosts (Lite)、AdGuard Base filter、AdGuard Base filter、AdGuard DNS filter、AdRules DNS List、Hblock、OISD Basic、1024 hosts、ad-wars hosts、StevenBlack hosts、xinggsf、EasyList、Easylist China、EasyPrivacy、CJX's Annoyance List、SmartTV Blocklist、AWAvenue Ads Rule、jiekouAD。Lite 版仅针对国内域名拦截。
